On the fourth day of our stay, we were called downstairs at 11 noon to ask if we needed to extend our room. Then we both said we wanted to extend our room. But when we came down to extend our room, they told us that there were only suites and no rooms. Moreover, I initially I paid 5,000 for pre-authorization and told them to extend our room without checking out. This kind of service is really very poor. You can consider several hotels nearby.
